114  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SHAMIR
115  static int s_ecc_test_shamir(void)
116  {
117     void *a, *modulus, *mp, *kA, *kB, *rA, *rB;
118     void *mu, *ma;
119     ecc_point *G, *A, *B, *C1, *C2;
120     int x, y, z;
121     unsigned char buf[ECC_BUF_SIZE];
122     DO(mp_init_multi(&kA, &kB, &rA, &rB, &modulus, &a, &mu, &ma, LTC_NULL));
123     LTC_ARGCHK((G  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
124     LTC_ARGCHK((A  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
125     LTC_ARGCHK((B  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
126     LTC_ARGCHK((C1 = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
127     LTC_ARGCHK((C2 = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
128     for (x = 0; x < (int)(sizeof(sizes)/sizeof(sizes[0])); x++) {
129         for (z = 0; ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime != NULL; z++) {
130             DO(mp_read_radix(modulus, ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime, 16));
131             if (sizes[x] <= mp_unsigned_bin_size(modulus)) break;
132         }
133         LTC_ARGCHK(ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime != NULL);
134         DO(mp_read_radix(G->x, ltc_ecc_curves[z].Gx, 16));
135         DO(mp_read_radix(G->y, ltc_ecc_curves[z].Gy, 16));
136         DO(mp_set(G->z, 1));
137         DO(mp_read_radix(a, ltc_ecc_curves[z].A, 16));
138         DO(mp_montgomery_setup(modulus, &mp));
139         DO(mp_montgomery_normalization(mu, modulus));
140         DO(mp_mulmod(a, mu, modulus, ma));
141         for (y = 0; y < 100; y++) {
142            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
143            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(rA, buf, sizes[x]));
144            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
145            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(rB, buf, sizes[x]));
146            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(rA, G, A, a, modulus, 1));
147            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(rB, G, B, a, modulus, 1));
148            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
149            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(kA, buf, sizes[x]));
150            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
151            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(kB, buf, sizes[x]));
152            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(kA, A, C1, a, modulus, 0));
153            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(kB, B, C2, a, modulus, 0));
154            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptadd(C1, C2, C1, a, modulus, mp));
155            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_map(C1, modulus, mp));
156            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_mul2add(A, kA, B, kB, C2, ma, modulus));
157            if ((mp_cmp(C1->x, C2->x) != LTC_MP_EQ) || (mp_cmp(C1->y, C2->y) != LTC_MP_EQ) || (mp_cmp(C1->z, C2->z) != LTC_MP_EQ)) {
158               fprintf(stderr, "ECC failed shamir test: size=%d, testno=%d\n", sizes[x], y);
159               return 1;
160            }
161        }
162        mp_montgomery_free(mp);
163    }
164    ltc_ecc_del_point(C2);
165    ltc_ecc_del_point(C1);
166    ltc_ecc_del_point(B);
167    ltc_ecc_del_point(A);
168    ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
169    mp_clear_multi(kA, kB, rA, rB, modulus, a, mu, ma, LTC_NULL);
170    return 0;
171  }

173  static int s_ecc_issue108(void)
174  {
175     void      *a, *modulus, *order;
176     ecc_point *Q, *Result;
177     int       err;
178     const ltc_ecc_curve* dp;
179     if ((err = mp_init_multi(&modulus, &order, &a, LTC_NULL)) != CRYPT_OK) { return err; }
180     Q      = ltc_ecc_new_point();
181     Result = ltc_ecc_new_point();
182     if ((err = ecc_find_curve("SECP224R1", &dp)) != CRYPT_OK)              { goto done; }
183     if ((err = mp_read_radix(a, (char *)dp->A,  16)) != CRYPT_OK)          { goto done; }
184     if ((err = mp_read_radix(modulus, (char *)dp->prime, 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
185     if ((err = mp_read_radix(order, (char *)dp->order, 16)) != CRYPT_OK)   { goto done; }
186     if ((err = mp_read_radix(Q->x, (char *)"EA3745501BBC6A70BBFDD8AEEDB18CF5073C6DC9AA7CBB5915170D60", 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
187     if ((err = mp_read_radix(Q->y, (char *)"6C9CB8E68AABFEC989CAC5E2326E0448B7E69C3E56039BA21A44FDAC", 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
188     mp_set(Q->z, 1);
189     if ((err = ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(order, Q, Result, a, modulus, 1)) != CRYPT_OK)  { goto done; }
190  done:
191     ltc_ecc_del_point(Result);
192     ltc_ecc_del_point(Q);
193     mp_clear_multi(modulus, order, a, LTC_NULL);
194     return err;
195  }

240  static int s_ecc_test_mp(void)
241  {
242     void       *a, *modulus, *order;
243     ecc_point  *G, *GG;
244     int        i, err, primality;
245     char buf[4096];
246     DO(mp_init_multi(&modulus, &order, &a, LTC_NULL));
247     G   = ltc_ecc_new_point();
248     GG  = ltc_ecc_new_point();
249     if (G == NULL || GG == NULL) {
250        mp_clear_multi(modulus, order, LTC_NULL);
251        ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
252        ltc_ecc_del_point(GG);
253        return CRYPT_MEM;
254     }
255     err = CRYPT_OK;
256     for (i = 0; ltc_ecc_curves[i].prime != NULL; i++) {
257        DO(mp_read_radix(a, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].A,  16));
258        DO(mp_read_radix(modulus, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].prime, 16));
259        DO(mp_read_radix(order, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].order, 16));
260        DO(mp_prime_is_prime(modulus, 8, &primality));
261        if (primality == 0) {
262           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
263           mp_tohex(modulus, buf);
264           printf("Modulus failed prime check: %s\n", buf);
265        }
266        DO(mp_prime_is_prime(order, 8, &primality));
267        if (primality == 0) {
268           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
269           mp_tohex(order, buf);
270           printf("Order failed prime check: %s\n", buf);
271        }
272        DO(mp_read_radix(G->x, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].Gx, 16));
273        DO(mp_read_radix(G->y, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].Gy, 16));
274        mp_set(G->z, 1);
275        DO(mp_add_d(order, 1, order));
276        DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(order, G, GG, a, modulus, 1));
277        if (mp_cmp(G->x, GG->x) != LTC_MP_EQ || mp_cmp(G->y, GG->y) != LTC_MP_EQ) {
278           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
279        }
280        if (err != CRYPT_OK) {
281           goto done;
282        }
283     }
284     err = CRYPT_OK;
285  done:
286     ltc_ecc_del_point(GG);
287     ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
288     mp_clear_multi(order, modulus, a, LTC_NULL);
289     return err;
290  }
291  static int s_ecc_old_api(void)
292  {
293     unsigned char buf[4][4096], ch;
294     unsigned long x, y, z, s;
295     int           stat, stat2;
296     ecc_key usera, userb, pubKey, privKey;
297     int low, high;
298     ecc_sizes(&low, &high);
299     if (low < 14 || high < 14 || low > 100 || high > 100 || high < low) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
300     for (s = 0; s < (sizeof(sizes)/sizeof(sizes[0])); s++) {
301        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &usera));
302        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &userb));
303        if (ecc_get_size(&usera) != (int)sizes[s]) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
304        if (ecc_get_size(&userb) != (int)sizes[s]) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
305        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
306        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[0], &x));
307        y = sizeof(buf[1]);
308        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&userb, &usera, buf[1], &y));
309        DO(do_compare_testvector(buf[0], x, buf[1], y, "ecc Shared keys", s));
310        y = sizeof(buf[0]);
311        DO(ecc_export (buf[1], &y, PK_PUBLIC, &userb));
312        ecc_free (&userb);
313        DO(ecc_import (buf[1], y, &userb));
314        z = sizeof(buf[0]);
315        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[2], &z));
316        if (z != x) {
317          fprintf(stderr, "failed.  Size don't match?");
318          return 1;
319        }
320        if (memcmp (buf[0], buf[2], x)) {
321          fprintf(stderr, "Failed.  Contents didn't match.");
322          return 1;
323        }
324        y = sizeof(buf[1]);
325        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_export(&userb, buf[1], &y));
326        ecc_free (&userb);
327        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_import(buf[1], y, &userb));
328        z = sizeof(buf[0]);
329        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[2], &z));
330        if (z != x) {
331          fprintf(stderr, "failed.  Size don't match?");
332          return 1;
333        }
334        if (memcmp (buf[0], buf[2], x)) {
335          fprintf(stderr, "Failed.  Contents didn't match.");
336          return 1;
337        }
338        ecc_free (&usera);
339        ecc_free (&userb);
340        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &usera));
341        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
342        DO(ecc_export(buf[0], &x, PK_PUBLIC, &usera));
343        DO(ecc_import(buf[0], x, &pubKey));
344        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
345        DO(ecc_export(buf[0], &x, PK_PRIVATE, &usera));
346        DO(ecc_import(buf[0], x, &privKey));
347        for (ch = 0; ch < 32; ch++) {
348           buf[0][ch] = ch;
349        }
350        y = sizeof (buf[1]);
351        DO(ecc_encrypt_key (buf[0], 32, buf[1], &y, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), find_hash ("sha256"), &pubKey));
352        zeromem (buf[0], sizeof (buf[0]));
353        x = sizeof (buf[0]);
354        DO(ecc_decrypt_key (buf[1], y, buf[0], &x, &privKey));
355        if (x != 32) {
356          fprintf(stderr, "Failed (length)");
357          return 1;
358        }
359        for (ch = 0; ch < 32; ch++) {
360           if (buf[0][ch] != ch) {
361              fprintf(stderr, "Failed (contents)");
362              return 1;
363           }
364        }
365        for (ch = 0; ch < 16; ch++) {
366           buf[0][ch] = ch;
367        }
368        x = sizeof (buf[1]);
369        DO(ecc_sign_hash (buf[0], 16, buf[1], &x, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privKey));
370        DO(ecc_verify_hash (buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat, &pubKey));
371        buf[0][0] ^= 1;
372        DO(ecc_verify_hash (buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat2, &privKey));
373        if (!(stat == 1 && stat2 == 0)) {
374           fprintf(stderr, "ecc_verify_hash failed %d, %d, ", stat, stat2);
375           return 1;
376        }
377        for (ch = 0; ch < 16; ch++) {
378           buf[0][ch] = ch;
379        }
380        x = sizeof (buf[1]);
381        DO(ecc_sign_hash_rfc7518(buf[0], 16, buf[1], &x, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privKey));
382        DO(ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518(buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat, &pubKey));
383        buf[0][0] ^= 1;
384        DO(ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518(buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat2, &privKey));
385        if (!(stat == 1 && stat2 == 0)) {
386           fprintf(stderr, "ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518 failed %d, %d, ", stat, stat2);
387           return 1;
388        }
389        ecc_free (&usera);
390        ecc_free (&pubKey);
391        ecc_free (&privKey);
392     }
393     return CRYPT_OK;
394  }
395  static int s_ecc_key_cmp(const int should_type, const ecc_key *should, const ecc_key *is)
396  {
397     if (should_type != is->type)                               return CRYPT_ERROR;
398     if (should_type == PK_PRIVATE) {
399        if (mp_cmp(should->k, is->k) != LTC_MP_EQ)              return CRYPT_ERROR;
400     }
401     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.prime,  is->dp.prime)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
402     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.A,      is->dp.A)      != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
403     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.B,      is->dp.B)      != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
404     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.order,  is->dp.order)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
405     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.base.x, is->dp.base.x) != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
406     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.base.y, is->dp.base.y) != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
407     if (mp_cmp(should->pubkey.x,  is->pubkey.x)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
408     if (mp_cmp(should->pubkey.y,  is->pubkey.y)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
409     if (should->dp.size != is->dp.size)                        return CRYPT_ERROR;
410     if (should->dp.cofactor != is->dp.cofactor)                return CRYPT_ERROR;
411     return CRYPT_OK;
412  }
413  static int s_ecc_new_api(void)
414  {
415     int i, j, stat;
416     const ltc_ecc_curve* dp;
417     ecc_key key, privkey, pubkey;
418     unsigned char buf[1000];
419     unsigned long len;
420     unsigned char data16[16] = { 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1 };
421     unsigned long len16;
422     for (i = 0; i < (int)(sizeof(curvenames)/sizeof(curvenames[0])); i++) {
423        DO(ecc_find_curve(curvenames[i], &dp));
424        DO(ecc_make_key_ex(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key, dp));
425        len = sizeof(buf);
426        DO(ecc_export(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
427        DO(ecc_import_ex(buf, len, &privkey, dp));
428        ecc_free(&privkey);
429        len = sizeof(buf);
430        DO(ecc_export(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &key));
431        DO(ecc_import_ex(buf, len, &pubkey, dp));
432        ecc_free(&pubkey);
433        len = sizeof(buf);
434        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_export(&key, buf, &len));
435        ecc_free(&key);
436        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_import_ex(buf, len, &pubkey, dp));
437        ecc_free(&pubkey);
438        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &key));
439        DO(ecc_generate_key(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key));
440        len = sizeof(buf);
441        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
442        ecc_free(&key);
443        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &privkey));
444        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PRIVATE, &privkey));
445        if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") != 0) {
446           len = sizeof(buf);
447           DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC|PK_COMPRESSED, &privkey));
448           if (len != 1 + (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
449           DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
450           DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
451           ecc_free(&pubkey);
452        }
453        len = sizeof(buf);
454        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &privkey));
455        if (len != 1 + 2 * (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
456        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
457        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
458        len = sizeof(buf);
459        DO(ecc_sign_hash(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privkey));
460        stat = 0;
461        DO(ecc_verify_hash(buf, len, data16, 16, &stat, &pubkey));
462        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
463  #ifdef LTC_SSH
464        len = sizeof(buf);
465        DO(ecc_sign_hash_ex(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"),
466                            LTC_ECCSIG_RFC5656, NULL, &privkey));
467        stat = 0;
468        DO(ecc_verify_hash_ex(buf, len, data16, 16, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC5656, &stat, &pubkey));
469        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
470  #endif
471  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SHAMIR
472        if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") != 0) {
473           int found = 0;
474           ecc_key reckey;
475           len = sizeof(buf);
476           DO(ecc_sign_hash(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privkey));
477           DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
478           for (j = 0; j < 2*(1+(int)privkey.dp.cofactor); j++) {
479              stat = ecc_recover_key(buf, len, data16, 16, j, LTC_ECCSIG_ANSIX962, &reckey);
480              if (stat != CRYPT_OK) continue; \* last two will almost always fail, only possible if x<(prime mod order) */
481              stat = s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey);
482              if (stat == CRYPT_OK) found++;
483           }
484           if (found != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR; \* unique match */
485           ecc_free(&reckey);
486        }
487  #endif
488        len = sizeof(buf);
489        DO(ecc_encrypt_key(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng("yarrow"), find_hash("sha256"), &pubkey));
490        zeromem(data16, 16);
491        len16 = 16;
492        DO(ecc_decrypt_key(buf, len, data16, &len16, &privkey));
493        if (len16 != 16) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
494        for (j = 0; j < 16; j++) if (data16[j] != 0xd1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
495        ecc_free(&privkey);
496        ecc_free(&pubkey);
497     }
498     return CRYPT_OK;
499  }

1309  static int s_ecc_test_recovery(void)
1310  {
1311     int i, recid, stat;
1312     const ltc_ecc_curve* dp;
1313     ecc_key key, privkey, pubkey, reckey;
1314     unsigned char buf[1000];
1315     unsigned long len;
1316     unsigned char data16[16] = { 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1 };
1317     unsigned char eth_hash[] = { \* Keccak-256 hash of "Hello World" */
1318        0x59, 0x2f, 0xa7, 0x43, 0x88, 0x9f, 0xc7, 0xf9, 0x2a, 0xc2, 0xa3, 0x7b, 0xb1, 0xf5, 0xba, 0x1d,
1319        0xaf, 0x2a, 0x5c, 0x84, 0x74, 0x1c, 0xa0, 0xe0, 0x06, 0x1d, 0x24, 0x3a, 0x2e, 0x67, 0x07, 0xba
1320     };
1321     unsigned char eth_pubkey[] = { \* Public part of randomly-generated key pair */
1322        0x04,
1323        0xc6, 0x99, 0x5f, 0xdc, 0xf4, 0xf2, 0xda, 0x6e, 0x79, 0xe0, 0x47, 0x12, 0xd3, 0xbe, 0x22, 0xe7,
1324        0x65, 0xc6, 0xa3, 0x32, 0x89, 0x1b, 0x34, 0xba, 0xc1, 0xb7, 0x01, 0x83, 0xed, 0xdd, 0xf1, 0xcc,
1325        0xbf, 0x20, 0xdd, 0xcd, 0x05, 0x4e, 0x49, 0xc8, 0xcb, 0x66, 0x6c, 0xb7, 0x71, 0x2f, 0x7e, 0xc1,
1326        0xd6, 0x1a, 0x4a, 0x42, 0x3d, 0xe5, 0xc2, 0x8d, 0x74, 0x03, 0x81, 0xe7, 0xea, 0xc5, 0x3c, 0x10
1327     };
1328     unsigned char eth_sig[] = { \* Signature of eth_hash to be verified against eth_pubkey */
1329        0xbd, 0x6d, 0xbb, 0xbe, 0x2d, 0xe7, 0x1d, 0x00, 0xae, 0x18, 0x57, 0x12, 0x1d, 0x63, 0xa5, 0x1b,
1330        0x0b, 0x42, 0x71, 0xa2, 0x80, 0x49, 0xe0, 0x5c, 0xfa, 0xc8, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x8a, 0x88, 0x67, 0x56,
1331        0xf6, 0x67, 0x1b, 0x41, 0x46, 0x09, 0x4e, 0xd0, 0x44, 0x25, 0x18, 0xfd, 0xf4, 0xcd, 0x62, 0xa3,
1332        0xb7, 0x3c, 0x97, 0x55, 0xfa, 0x69, 0xf8, 0xef, 0xe9, 0xcf, 0x12, 0xaf, 0x48, 0x25, 0xe3, 0xe0,
1333        0x1b
1334     };
1335     if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") == 0) return CRYPT_NOP;
1336  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SECP256K1
1337     DO(ecc_find_curve("SECP256K1", &dp));
1338     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
1339     DO(ecc_set_key(eth_pubkey, sizeof(eth_pubkey), PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
1340     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1341     stat = ecc_recover_key(eth_sig, sizeof(eth_sig)-1, eth_hash, sizeof(eth_hash), 0, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &reckey);
1342     if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1343     DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1344     ecc_free(&reckey);
1345     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1346     stat = ecc_recover_key(eth_sig, sizeof(eth_sig), eth_hash, sizeof(eth_hash), -1, LTC_ECCSIG_ETH27, &reckey);
1347     if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1348     DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1349     ecc_free(&reckey);
1350     ecc_free(&pubkey);
1351  #endif
1352     for (i = 0; i < (int)(sizeof(curvenames)/sizeof(curvenames[0])); i++) {
1353        DO(ecc_find_curve(curvenames[i], &dp));
1354        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &key));
1355        DO(ecc_generate_key(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key));
1356        len = sizeof(buf);
1357        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
1358        ecc_free(&key);
1359        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &privkey));
1360        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PRIVATE, &privkey));
1361        len = sizeof(buf);
1362        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &privkey));
1363        if (len != 1 + 2 * (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1364        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
1365        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
1366        len = sizeof(buf);
1367        recid = 0;
1368        DO(ecc_sign_hash_ex(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &recid, &privkey));
1369        stat = 0;
1370        DO(ecc_verify_hash_ex(buf, len, data16, 16, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &stat, &pubkey));
1371        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1372        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1373        stat = ecc_recover_key(buf, len, data16, 16, recid, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &reckey);
1374        if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1375        DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1376        ecc_free(&reckey);
1377        ecc_free(&privkey);
1378        ecc_free(&pubkey);
1379     }
1380    return CRYPT_OK;
1381  }
1382  #endif
1383  int ecc_test(void)
1384  {
1385     if (ltc_mp.name == NULL) return CRYPT_NOP;
1386     DO(s_ecc_old_api()); \* up to 1.18 */
1387     DO(s_ecc_new_api());
1388     DO(s_ecc_import_export());
1389     DO(s_ecc_test_mp());
1390     DO(s_ecc_issue108());
1391     DO(s_ecc_issue443_447());
1392  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SHAMIR
1393     DO(s_ecc_test_shamir());
1394     DO(s_ecc_test_recovery());
1395  #endif
1396     return CRYPT_OK;
1397  }

114  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SHAMIR
115  static int s_ecc_test_shamir(void)
116  {
117     void *a, *modulus, *mp, *kA, *kB, *rA, *rB;
118     void *mu, *ma;
119     ecc_point *G, *A, *B, *C1, *C2;
120     int x, y, z;
121     unsigned char buf[ECC_BUF_SIZE];
122     DO(mp_init_multi(&kA, &kB, &rA, &rB, &modulus, &a, &mu, &ma, LTC_NULL));
123     LTC_ARGCHK((G  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
124     LTC_ARGCHK((A  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
125     LTC_ARGCHK((B  = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
126     LTC_ARGCHK((C1 = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
127     LTC_ARGCHK((C2 = ltc_ecc_new_point()) != NULL);
128     for (x = 0; x < (int)(sizeof(sizes)/sizeof(sizes[0])); x++) {
129         for (z = 0; ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime != NULL; z++) {
130             DO(mp_read_radix(modulus, ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime, 16));
131             if (sizes[x] <= mp_unsigned_bin_size(modulus)) break;
132         }
133         LTC_ARGCHK(ltc_ecc_curves[z].prime != NULL);
134         DO(mp_read_radix(G->x, ltc_ecc_curves[z].Gx, 16));
135         DO(mp_read_radix(G->y, ltc_ecc_curves[z].Gy, 16));
136         DO(mp_set(G->z, 1));
137         DO(mp_read_radix(a, ltc_ecc_curves[z].A, 16));
138         DO(mp_montgomery_setup(modulus, &mp));
139         DO(mp_montgomery_normalization(mu, modulus));
140         DO(mp_mulmod(a, mu, modulus, ma));
141         for (y = 0; y < 100; y++) {
142            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
143            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(rA, buf, sizes[x]));
144            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
145            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(rB, buf, sizes[x]));
146            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(rA, G, A, a, modulus, 1));
147            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(rB, G, B, a, modulus, 1));
148            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
149            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(kA, buf, sizes[x]));
150            ENSURE(yarrow_read(buf, sizes[x], &yarrow_prng) == sizes[x]);
151            DO(mp_read_unsigned_bin(kB, buf, sizes[x]));
152            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(kA, A, C1, a, modulus, 0));
153            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(kB, B, C2, a, modulus, 0));
154            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptadd(C1, C2, C1, a, modulus, mp));
155            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_map(C1, modulus, mp));
156            DO(ltc_mp.ecc_mul2add(A, kA, B, kB, C2, ma, modulus));
157            if ((mp_cmp(C1->x, C2->x) != LTC_MP_EQ) || (mp_cmp(C1->y, C2->y) != LTC_MP_EQ) || (mp_cmp(C1->z, C2->z) != LTC_MP_EQ)) {
158               fprintf(stderr, "ECC failed shamir test: size=%d, testno=%d\n", sizes[x], y);
159               return 1;
160            }
161        }
162        mp_montgomery_free(mp);
163    }
164    ltc_ecc_del_point(C2);
165    ltc_ecc_del_point(C1);
166    ltc_ecc_del_point(B);
167    ltc_ecc_del_point(A);
168    ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
169    mp_clear_multi(kA, kB, rA, rB, modulus, a, mu, ma, LTC_NULL);
170    return 0;
171  }
172  #endif
173  static int s_ecc_issue108(void)
174  {
175     void      *a, *modulus, *order;
176     ecc_point *Q, *Result;
177     int       err;
178     const ltc_ecc_curve* dp;
179     if ((err = mp_init_multi(&modulus, &order, &a, LTC_NULL)) != CRYPT_OK) { return err; }
180     Q      = ltc_ecc_new_point();
181     Result = ltc_ecc_new_point();
182     if ((err = ecc_find_curve("SECP224R1", &dp)) != CRYPT_OK)              { goto done; }
183     if ((err = mp_read_radix(a, (char *)dp->A,  16)) != CRYPT_OK)          { goto done; }
184     if ((err = mp_read_radix(modulus, (char *)dp->prime, 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
185     if ((err = mp_read_radix(order, (char *)dp->order, 16)) != CRYPT_OK)   { goto done; }
186     if ((err = mp_read_radix(Q->x, (char *)"EA3745501BBC6A70BBFDD8AEEDB18CF5073C6DC9AA7CBB5915170D60", 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
187     if ((err = mp_read_radix(Q->y, (char *)"6C9CB8E68AABFEC989CAC5E2326E0448B7E69C3E56039BA21A44FDAC", 16)) != CRYPT_OK) { goto done; }
188     mp_set(Q->z, 1);
189     if ((err = ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(order, Q, Result, a, modulus, 1)) != CRYPT_OK)  { goto done; }
190  done:
191     ltc_ecc_del_point(Result);
192     ltc_ecc_del_point(Q);
193     mp_clear_multi(modulus, order, a, LTC_NULL);
194     return err;
195  }

240  static int s_ecc_test_mp(void)
241  {
242     void       *a, *modulus, *order;
243     ecc_point  *G, *GG;
244     int        i, err, primality;
245     char buf[4096];
246     DO(mp_init_multi(&modulus, &order, &a, LTC_NULL));
247     G   = ltc_ecc_new_point();
248     GG  = ltc_ecc_new_point();
249     if (G == NULL || GG == NULL) {
250        mp_clear_multi(modulus, order, LTC_NULL);
251        ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
252        ltc_ecc_del_point(GG);
253        return CRYPT_MEM;
254     }
255     err = CRYPT_OK;
256     for (i = 0; ltc_ecc_curves[i].prime != NULL; i++) {
257        DO(mp_read_radix(a, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].A,  16));
258        DO(mp_read_radix(modulus, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].prime, 16));
259        DO(mp_read_radix(order, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].order, 16));
260        DO(mp_prime_is_prime(modulus, 8, &primality));
261        if (primality == 0) {
262           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
263           mp_tohex(modulus, buf);
264           printf("Modulus failed prime check: %s\n", buf);
265        }
266        DO(mp_prime_is_prime(order, 8, &primality));
267        if (primality == 0) {
268           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
269           mp_tohex(order, buf);
270           printf("Order failed prime check: %s\n", buf);
271        }
272        DO(mp_read_radix(G->x, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].Gx, 16));
273        DO(mp_read_radix(G->y, (char *)ltc_ecc_curves[i].Gy, 16));
274        mp_set(G->z, 1);
275        DO(mp_add_d(order, 1, order));
276        DO(ltc_mp.ecc_ptmul(order, G, GG, a, modulus, 1));
277        if (mp_cmp(G->x, GG->x) != LTC_MP_EQ || mp_cmp(G->y, GG->y) != LTC_MP_EQ) {
278           err = CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
279        }
280        if (err != CRYPT_OK) {
281           goto done;
282        }
283     }
284     err = CRYPT_OK;
285  done:
286     ltc_ecc_del_point(GG);
287     ltc_ecc_del_point(G);
288     mp_clear_multi(order, modulus, a, LTC_NULL);
289     return err;
290  }
291  static int s_ecc_old_api(void)
292  {
293     unsigned char buf[4][4096], ch;
294     unsigned long x, y, z, s;
295     int           stat, stat2;
296     ecc_key usera, userb, pubKey, privKey;
297     int low, high;
298     ecc_sizes(&low, &high);
299     if (low < 14 || high < 14 || low > 100 || high > 100 || high < low) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
300     for (s = 0; s < (sizeof(sizes)/sizeof(sizes[0])); s++) {
301        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &usera));
302        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &userb));
303        if (ecc_get_size(&usera) != (int)sizes[s]) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
304        if (ecc_get_size(&userb) != (int)sizes[s]) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
305        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
306        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[0], &x));
307        y = sizeof(buf[1]);
308        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&userb, &usera, buf[1], &y));
309        DO(do_compare_testvector(buf[0], x, buf[1], y, "ecc Shared keys", s));
310        y = sizeof(buf[0]);
311        DO(ecc_export (buf[1], &y, PK_PUBLIC, &userb));
312        ecc_free (&userb);
313        DO(ecc_import (buf[1], y, &userb));
314        z = sizeof(buf[0]);
315        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[2], &z));
316        if (z != x) {
317          fprintf(stderr, "failed.  Size don't match?");
318          return 1;
319        }
320        if (memcmp (buf[0], buf[2], x)) {
321          fprintf(stderr, "Failed.  Contents didn't match.");
322          return 1;
323        }
324        y = sizeof(buf[1]);
325        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_export(&userb, buf[1], &y));
326        ecc_free (&userb);
327        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_import(buf[1], y, &userb));
328        z = sizeof(buf[0]);
329        DO(ecc_shared_secret (&usera, &userb, buf[2], &z));
330        if (z != x) {
331          fprintf(stderr, "failed.  Size don't match?");
332          return 1;
333        }
334        if (memcmp (buf[0], buf[2], x)) {
335          fprintf(stderr, "Failed.  Contents didn't match.");
336          return 1;
337        }
338        ecc_free (&usera);
339        ecc_free (&userb);
340        DO(ecc_make_key (&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), sizes[s], &usera));
341        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
342        DO(ecc_export(buf[0], &x, PK_PUBLIC, &usera));
343        DO(ecc_import(buf[0], x, &pubKey));
344        x = sizeof(buf[0]);
345        DO(ecc_export(buf[0], &x, PK_PRIVATE, &usera));
346        DO(ecc_import(buf[0], x, &privKey));
347        for (ch = 0; ch < 32; ch++) {
348           buf[0][ch] = ch;
349        }
350        y = sizeof (buf[1]);
351        DO(ecc_encrypt_key (buf[0], 32, buf[1], &y, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), find_hash ("sha256"), &pubKey));
352        zeromem (buf[0], sizeof (buf[0]));
353        x = sizeof (buf[0]);
354        DO(ecc_decrypt_key (buf[1], y, buf[0], &x, &privKey));
355        if (x != 32) {
356          fprintf(stderr, "Failed (length)");
357          return 1;
358        }
359        for (ch = 0; ch < 32; ch++) {
360           if (buf[0][ch] != ch) {
361              fprintf(stderr, "Failed (contents)");
362              return 1;
363           }
364        }
365        for (ch = 0; ch < 16; ch++) {
366           buf[0][ch] = ch;
367        }
368        x = sizeof (buf[1]);
369        DO(ecc_sign_hash (buf[0], 16, buf[1], &x, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privKey));
370        DO(ecc_verify_hash (buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat, &pubKey));
371        buf[0][0] ^= 1;
372        DO(ecc_verify_hash (buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat2, &privKey));
373        if (!(stat == 1 && stat2 == 0)) {
374           fprintf(stderr, "ecc_verify_hash failed %d, %d, ", stat, stat2);
375           return 1;
376        }
377        for (ch = 0; ch < 16; ch++) {
378           buf[0][ch] = ch;
379        }
380        x = sizeof (buf[1]);
381        DO(ecc_sign_hash_rfc7518(buf[0], 16, buf[1], &x, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privKey));
382        DO(ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518(buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat, &pubKey));
383        buf[0][0] ^= 1;
384        DO(ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518(buf[1], x, buf[0], 16, &stat2, &privKey));
385        if (!(stat == 1 && stat2 == 0)) {
386           fprintf(stderr, "ecc_verify_hash_rfc7518 failed %d, %d, ", stat, stat2);
387           return 1;
388        }
389        ecc_free (&usera);
390        ecc_free (&pubKey);
391        ecc_free (&privKey);
392     }
393     return CRYPT_OK;
394  }
395  static int s_ecc_key_cmp(const int should_type, const ecc_key *should, const ecc_key *is)
396  {
397     if (should_type != is->type)                               return CRYPT_ERROR;
398     if (should_type == PK_PRIVATE) {
399        if (mp_cmp(should->k, is->k) != LTC_MP_EQ)              return CRYPT_ERROR;
400     }
401     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.prime,  is->dp.prime)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
402     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.A,      is->dp.A)      != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
403     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.B,      is->dp.B)      != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
404     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.order,  is->dp.order)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
405     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.base.x, is->dp.base.x) != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
406     if (mp_cmp(should->dp.base.y, is->dp.base.y) != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
407     if (mp_cmp(should->pubkey.x,  is->pubkey.x)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
408     if (mp_cmp(should->pubkey.y,  is->pubkey.y)  != LTC_MP_EQ) return CRYPT_ERROR;
409     if (should->dp.size != is->dp.size)                        return CRYPT_ERROR;
410     if (should->dp.cofactor != is->dp.cofactor)                return CRYPT_ERROR;
411     return CRYPT_OK;
412  }
413  static int s_ecc_new_api(void)
414  {
415     int i, j, stat;
416     const ltc_ecc_curve* dp;
417     ecc_key key, privkey, pubkey;
418     unsigned char buf[1000];
419     unsigned long len;
420     unsigned char data16[16] = { 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1, 0xd1 };
421     unsigned long len16;
422     for (i = 0; i < (int)(sizeof(curvenames)/sizeof(curvenames[0])); i++) {
423        DO(ecc_find_curve(curvenames[i], &dp));
424        DO(ecc_make_key_ex(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key, dp));
425        len = sizeof(buf);
426        DO(ecc_export(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
427        DO(ecc_import_ex(buf, len, &privkey, dp));
428        ecc_free(&privkey);
429        len = sizeof(buf);
430        DO(ecc_export(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &key));
431        DO(ecc_import_ex(buf, len, &pubkey, dp));
432        ecc_free(&pubkey);
433        len = sizeof(buf);
434        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_export(&key, buf, &len));
435        ecc_free(&key);
436        DO(ecc_ansi_x963_import_ex(buf, len, &pubkey, dp));
437        ecc_free(&pubkey);
438        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &key));
439        DO(ecc_generate_key(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key));
440        len = sizeof(buf);
441        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
442        ecc_free(&key);
443        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &privkey));
444        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PRIVATE, &privkey));
445        if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") != 0) {
446           len = sizeof(buf);
447           DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC|PK_COMPRESSED, &privkey));
448           if (len != 1 + (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
449           DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
450           DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
451           ecc_free(&pubkey);
452        }
453        len = sizeof(buf);
454        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &privkey));
455        if (len != 1 + 2 * (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
456        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
457        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
458        len = sizeof(buf);
459        DO(ecc_sign_hash(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privkey));
460        stat = 0;
461        DO(ecc_verify_hash(buf, len, data16, 16, &stat, &pubkey));
462        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
463  #ifdef LTC_SSH
464        len = sizeof(buf);
465        DO(ecc_sign_hash_ex(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"),
466                            LTC_ECCSIG_RFC5656, NULL, &privkey));
467        stat = 0;
468        DO(ecc_verify_hash_ex(buf, len, data16, 16, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC5656, &stat, &pubkey));
469        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
470  #endif
471  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SHAMIR
472        if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") != 0) {
473           int found = 0;
474           ecc_key reckey;
475           len = sizeof(buf);
476           DO(ecc_sign_hash(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &privkey));
477           DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
478           for (j = 0; j < 2*(1+(int)privkey.dp.cofactor); j++) {
479              stat = ecc_recover_key(buf, len, data16, 16, j, LTC_ECCSIG_ANSIX962, &reckey);
480              if (stat != CRYPT_OK) continue; \* last two will almost always fail, only possible if x<(prime mod order) */
481              stat = s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey);
482              if (stat == CRYPT_OK) found++;
483           }
484           if (found != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR; \* unique match */
485           ecc_free(&reckey);
486        }
487  #endif
488        len = sizeof(buf);
489        DO(ecc_encrypt_key(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng("yarrow"), find_hash("sha256"), &pubkey));
490        zeromem(data16, 16);
491        len16 = 16;
492        DO(ecc_decrypt_key(buf, len, data16, &len16, &privkey));
493        if (len16 != 16) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
494        for (j = 0; j < 16; j++) if (data16[j] != 0xd1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
495        ecc_free(&privkey);
496        ecc_free(&pubkey);
497     }
498     return CRYPT_OK;
499  }

1142     if (ltc_mp.sqrtmod_prime == NULL) return CRYPT_NOP; \* we need compressed points which requires sqrtmod_prime */
1143     DO(ecc_import_openssl(short_pub, sizeof(short_pub), &pub));
1144     DO(ecc_import_openssl(short_pri, sizeof(short_pri), &pri));
1145     DO(ecc_find_curve("SECP256K1", &cu));
1146     DO(ecc_set_curve(cu, &key));
1147     DO(ecc_set_key(raw_pri, sizeof(raw_pri),  PK_PRIVATE, &key));
1148     DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PRIVATE, &pri, &key));

1289     outlen = sizeof(out);

1292     outlen = sizeof(out);

1319        0xaf, 0x2a, 0x5c, 0x84, 0x74, 0x1c, 0xa0, 0xe0, 0x06, 0x1d, 0x24, 0x3a, 0x2e, 0x67, 0x07, 0xba
1320     };
1321     unsigned char eth_pubkey[] = { \* Public part of randomly-generated key pair */
1322        0x04,
1323        0xc6, 0x99, 0x5f, 0xdc, 0xf4, 0xf2, 0xda, 0x6e, 0x79, 0xe0, 0x47, 0x12, 0xd3, 0xbe, 0x22, 0xe7,
1324        0x65, 0xc6, 0xa3, 0x32, 0x89, 0x1b, 0x34, 0xba, 0xc1, 0xb7, 0x01, 0x83, 0xed, 0xdd, 0xf1, 0xcc,
1325        0xbf, 0x20, 0xdd, 0xcd, 0x05, 0x4e, 0x49, 0xc8, 0xcb, 0x66, 0x6c, 0xb7, 0x71, 0x2f, 0x7e, 0xc1,
1326        0xd6, 0x1a, 0x4a, 0x42, 0x3d, 0xe5, 0xc2, 0x8d, 0x74, 0x03, 0x81, 0xe7, 0xea, 0xc5, 0x3c, 0x10
1327     };
1328     unsigned char eth_sig[] = { \* Signature of eth_hash to be verified against eth_pubkey */
1329        0xbd, 0x6d, 0xbb, 0xbe, 0x2d, 0xe7, 0x1d, 0x00, 0xae, 0x18, 0x57, 0x12, 0x1d, 0x63, 0xa5, 0x1b,
1330        0x0b, 0x42, 0x71, 0xa2, 0x80, 0x49, 0xe0, 0x5c, 0xfa, 0xc8, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x8a, 0x88, 0x67, 0x56,
1331        0xf6, 0x67, 0x1b, 0x41, 0x46, 0x09, 0x4e, 0xd0, 0x44, 0x25, 0x18, 0xfd, 0xf4, 0xcd, 0x62, 0xa3,
1332        0xb7, 0x3c, 0x97, 0x55, 0xfa, 0x69, 0xf8, 0xef, 0xe9, 0xcf, 0x12, 0xaf, 0x48, 0x25, 0xe3, 0xe0,
1333        0x1b
1334     };
1335     if (strcmp(ltc_mp.name, "TomsFastMath") == 0) return CRYPT_NOP;
1336  #ifdef LTC_ECC_SECP256K1
1337     DO(ecc_find_curve("SECP256K1", &dp));
1338     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
1339     DO(ecc_set_key(eth_pubkey, sizeof(eth_pubkey), PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
1340     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1341     stat = ecc_recover_key(eth_sig, sizeof(eth_sig)-1, eth_hash, sizeof(eth_hash), 0, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &reckey);
1342     if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1343     DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1344     ecc_free(&reckey);
1345     DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1346     stat = ecc_recover_key(eth_sig, sizeof(eth_sig), eth_hash, sizeof(eth_hash), -1, LTC_ECCSIG_ETH27, &reckey);
1347     if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1348     DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1349     ecc_free(&reckey);
1350     ecc_free(&pubkey);
1351  #endif
1352     for (i = 0; i < (int)(sizeof(curvenames)/sizeof(curvenames[0])); i++) {
1353        DO(ecc_find_curve(curvenames[i], &dp));
1354        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &key));
1355        DO(ecc_generate_key(&yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), &key));
1356        len = sizeof(buf);
1357        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PRIVATE, &key));
1358        ecc_free(&key);
1359        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &privkey));
1360        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PRIVATE, &privkey));
1361        len = sizeof(buf);
1362        DO(ecc_get_key(buf, &len, PK_PUBLIC, &privkey));
1363        if (len != 1 + 2 * (unsigned)ecc_get_size(&privkey)) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1364        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &pubkey));
1365        DO(ecc_set_key(buf, len, PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey));
1366        len = sizeof(buf);
1367        recid = 0;
1368        DO(ecc_sign_hash_ex(data16, 16, buf, &len, &yarrow_prng, find_prng ("yarrow"), LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &recid, &privkey));
1369        stat = 0;
1370        DO(ecc_verify_hash_ex(buf, len, data16, 16, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &stat, &pubkey));
1371        if (stat != 1) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1372        DO(ecc_set_curve(dp, &reckey));
1373        stat = ecc_recover_key(buf, len, data16, 16, recid, LTC_ECCSIG_RFC7518, &reckey);
1374        if (stat != CRYPT_OK) return CRYPT_FAIL_TESTVECTOR;
1375        DO(s_ecc_key_cmp(PK_PUBLIC, &pubkey, &reckey));
1376        ecc_free(&reckey);
1377        ecc_free(&privkey);
1378        ecc_free(&pubkey);
1379     }
1380    return CRYPT_OK;
1381  }
